		$('document').ready(function(){
			function goToPage() {
				const val = $('#go-to-page').val();
				if(isNaN(val)) return;
				const tail = (val>1) ? '?p='+val : '';
				const url = `https://wallpapers.com/backgrounds`+tail;
				window.location = url;
			}
			$('#go-to-page').blur(goToPage);
			$('#go-to-page').on('keypress', function(e) {
				if(e.which == 13) {
					goToPage();
				}
			})});
